
<!-- README.md is generated from README.Rmd. Please edit that file -->

# Quality Checks

This repository includes the parametrized script to run Quality Checks
in R.

To use:

1.  Open the **project** QualityCheck

2.  Open the Rmd 00QualityCheck

Before running the script the following packages are required

To install

``` r
#For reading data
install.packages("here") #for assigning directory in a project
install.packages("readxl") #for reading excelsheet
install.packages("tidyverse") #for data wrangling
install.packages("beepr") #for making a noise when ready

#For report
install.packages("knitr") #for exporting tables in word
install.packages("kableExtra") #for arranging tables in word
install.packages("ggplot2") #for making plots
install.packages("sp") #for reading shapefiles
install.packages("sf") #for plotting shapefiles

install.packages("devtools")
devtools::install_github("MiriamLL/GermanNorthSea") #for loading shapefiles
devtools::install_github("MiriamLL/seamonas") #for accessing Euring information

#For Dinamic maps 
install.packages("tmap") #for creating maps with layers
install.packages("fontawesome") #for adding icons
```

## 00QualityCheck

### Reading the files

The script is about reading your data. It is parametrized that the data
should be in the folder 00Data, either copy your file to this folder, o
give the direction.

The sheets in the excelfile should be organized as: 1. Tripdaten 2.
Basisdaten 3. Observations Please provide this order and this names for
the sheets.

### Running the formal check validation

Basically, as it is an Rmd you would just need to run the script or
click on the green play (triangle) symbol to run.

#### 01FormalCheckandDataValidation

Checks that the column names are completely filled and that they fit
their expected names.  
It also checks that mandatory columns are fully filled, and for the
non-mandatory calculates how many where filled.  
Moreover, it checks which values were used in each column, and compares
with the expected values.

##### Trip Daten

Reproduce test data

``` r
library(tidyverse)

                       ENDTIME='11:00:00',

                       RESOLUTION=2,
                       PLANE_FLIGHT_HEIGHT_PLANNED=540,
                       STRIP_WIDTH=400,
                       PLANE_SPEED=100,

                       SCREENING_CONTROL_DIFFERENCE=15,
                       ID_CONTROL_DIFFERENCE=20,

                       POSITIONSYSTEM='GPS',
                       POSIT_PRECISION_CODE=1,
                       REFSYSTEM='WGS84',
                       NOTES=NA
                       )
```

``` r
BasisDaten_test<-BasisDaten_test %>%
  mutate(PIC_FILE_NAME=paste0("CAM",
                              CAMERA_NUMBER,"-",
                              rep(1:4, times=250),
                              rep(c("L","L","L","L","R","R","R","R"),times=125)))
```

``` r
BasisDaten_test$POSITION_ID_CONTROLLED[floor(runif(744, min=0, max=1000))]<-NA
BasisDaten_test$POSITION_ID_CONTROLLED[floor(runif(6, min=0, max=1000))]<-2
BasisDaten_test$POSITION_ID_CONTROLLED[floor(runif(3, min=0, max=1000))]<-3
```
